				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<div class="elementor-shortcode"><div id="pp-podcast-8316" class="pp-podcast has-header header-hidden has-featured playerview media-audio"  data-teaser="" data-elength="25" data-eunit=""><div class="pp-podcast__wrapper"><div class="pp-podcast__info pod-info"><div class="pod-info__header pod-header"><div class="pod-header__image"><div class="pod-header__image-wrapper"><img decoding="async" class="podcast-cover-image" src="https://pbcdn1.podbean.com/imglogo/image-logo/14080049/girlish_gurusbt2m5.jpg" srcset="" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 25vw" alt="Girlish Gurus"></div><span class="pod-header__image-style" style="display: block; width: 100%; padding-top: 100%"></div><div class="pod-header__items pod-items"><div class="pod-items__title">Girlish Gurus</div><div class="pod-items__desc"><p>Friends Joy &amp; Lorraine discuss a variety of topics that matter to women mid-life and beyond.  Thoughtful and engaging conversations covering everything from our overall wellbeing to creativity and travel.</p>
</div></div></div></div><div class="pp-podcast__content pod-content"><div class="pp-podcast__single"><div class="pp-podcast__player"><div class="pp-player-episode"><audio id="pp-podcast-8316-player" preload="none" class="pp-podcast-episode" style="width: 100%;" controls="controls"><source type="audio/mpeg" src="https://mcdn.podbean.com/mf/web/5ny8e3ejv9ufipte/2-21-26_Atessa_Bradley_edit_AUDIO9mxza.mp3" /></audio></div></div><div class="pod-content__episode episode-single"><button class="episode-single__close" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Close Single Episode"><span class="btn-icon-wrap"><svg class="icon icon-pp-x" aria-hidden="true" role="img" focusable="false"><use href="#icon-pp-x" xlink:href="#icon-pp-x"></use></svg></span></button><div class="episode-single__wrapper"><div class="episode-single__header"><div class="episode-single__title">Standing Tall with Attessa Bradley: How Purposeful Nutrition Helps Women Add Life to Their Years</div><div class="episode-single__author"><span class="byname">by</span><span class="single-author">girlishgurus</span></div></div><div class="episode-single__description"><p>What if one of the most powerful tools for midlife health was sitting right on your plate?</p><p>In this inspiring and informative episode, Joy and Lorraine sit down with Attessa Bradley, founder of Standing Tall Foods, to talk about purposeful nutrition for women in perimenopause and beyond. After her own wake-up call at age 49, Attessa discovered a massive gap in the way women’s health—and especially nutrition—was being addressed. That realization sparked a mission: to create convenient, nourishing foods designed specifically to help women add life to their years, not just years to their lives.</p><p>Together, we dive into the science, myths, and real-life challenges women face in midlife, and how simple nutritional shifts—especially increasing high-quality protein—can support bone health, heart health, brain function, and overall vitality.</p><p>If you’ve ever wondered whether you’re getting enough protein, felt confused about soy, or wanted more practical nutrition solutions designed with women in mind, this episode is for you.</p><p> </p><p>In This Episode, We Discuss:</p><ul><li>Attessa’s personal perimenopause wake-up call at age 49</li><li>The massive gap in women’s health and nutrition support</li><li>Why women are at higher risk for:<ul><li>Osteoporosis</li><li>Cardiovascular disease</li><li>Alzheimer’s disease</li></ul></li><li>The importance of purposeful nutrition in midlife</li><li>Why protein needs increase as we age</li><li>Common myths and misconceptions about soy</li><li>What the research actually says about soy and women’s health</li><li>Why Attessa chose soy as the hero ingredient in her product</li><li>How Standing Tall Foods was developed</li><li>What makes the product different from typical “healthy snacks”</li><li>The journey from idea to launch</li><li>The power of community support for women-founded brands</li></ul><p> </p><p>Key Takeaways</p><p>✨ Midlife nutrition is not just about weight—it’s about strength, brain health, and longevity.<br />✨ Women often need more protein as they age, not less.<br />✨ Many fears around soy are based on outdated or misunderstood information.<br />✨ Proactive nutrition can help reduce risks of osteoporosis, heart disease, and cognitive decline.<br />✨ It’s never too late to build something meaningful—or to take better care of yourself.</p><p> </p><p>About Our Guest</p><p>Attessa Bradley is the founder of Standing Tall Foods, created after her own perimenopause experience revealed how underserved women are when it comes to nutrition.</p><p>With over 25 years of experience building successful health-minded brands like Stonyfield, Orgain, Grandy Organics, and Church &amp; Dwight’s First Response, Attessa brings deep expertise in both business and women’s health. She holds an MBA from Thunderbird and is passionate about delivering powerful food for powerful women.</p><p> </p><p>Connect with Standing Tall Foods</p><ul><li><a href='https://standingtallfoods.com/'>Visit the website to learn more</a></li><li>Explore their products designed specifically for midlife women</li><li>Support a women-founded brand focused on proactive health</li></ul><p> </p><p>Share the Love</p><p>If this episode resonated with you:</p><ul><li>Share it with a friend, sister, or midlife buddy</li><li>Leave a review on your favorite podcast platform</li><li>Tag us on social media and tell us your biggest takeaway</li></ul><p>Because midlife isn’t the beginning of the end—<br />it’s the start of standing tall.</p><p> </p><p>RESOURCES MENTIONED IN THIS EPISODE:</p><p><a href='https://standingtallfoods.com/'>Standing Tall Foods</a></p><p><a href='https://discover.lifelinescreening.com/lmac/?sourcecd=LMAC625&amp;utm_source=ig&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_content=link_in_bio&amp;fbclid=PAZXh0bgNhZW0CMTEAc3J0YwZhcHBfaWQMMjU2MjgxMDQwNTU4AAGn2k-COFsgw99NzKf1v86f6d5F47c4xANgBApMvilReudyZzkomVgnDe5vUYY_aem_pL3H7bNHWWe3VHzcT7gP9A'>LIFE LINE SCREENING</a>: It’s American Health Month! Get Peace of Mind!</p><p>Follow us on YouTube: <a href='https://www.youtube.com/@girlishgurus'>Girlish Gurus</a></p><p>Follow us on Instagram: <a href='https://www.instagram.com/girlishgurus/'>@girlishgurus</a></p><p>Hashtags</p><p>#GirlishGurus #MidlifeMagic #MenopauseWellness #ProteinForWomen #HealthyAging #WomenSupportingWomen #PurposefulNutrition #MidlifeHealth #MenopauseSupport #WomensWellness</p></div></div><div class="ppjs__img-wrapper "><div class="ppjs__img-btn-cover"><img decoding="async" class="ppjs__img-btn" src="https://pbcdn1.podbean.com/imglogo/image-logo/14080049/girlish_gurusbt2m5.jpg" srcset="" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 300px" alt="Standing Tall with Attessa Bradley: How Purposeful Nutrition Helps Women Add Life to Their Years"></div><div><span class="ppjs__img-btn-style" style="display: block; width: 100%; padding-top: 100%"></div></div></div></div><div class="pod-content__list episode-list"><div class="episode-list__filters"><div class="episode-list__search"><label class="label-episode-search"><span class="ppjs__offscreen">Search Episodes</span><input type="text" placeholder="Search Episodes" title="Search Podcast Episodes"/></label><span class="episode-list__search-icon"><svg class="icon icon-pp-search" aria-hidden="true" role="img" focusable="false"><use href="#icon-pp-search" xlink:href="#icon-pp-search"></use></svg></span></div><button class="episode-list__clear-search pod-button"><svg class="icon icon-pp-x" aria-hidden="true" role="img" focusable="false"><use href="#icon-pp-x" xlink:href="#icon-pp-x"></use></svg><span class="ppjs__offscreen">Clear Search</span></button></div><div class="episode-list__wrapper">

                        $(this).val(0);

                    $input = $(this).prev('input.qty');
                    var val = parseInt($input.val());
                    var step = $input.attr('step');
                    step = 'undefined' !== typeof (step) ? parseInt(step) : 1;
                    $input.val(val + step).change();
                });
                $(document).on('click', '.minus',  // replace '.quantity' with document (without single quote)
                    function (e) {
                        $input = $(this).next('input.qty');
                        var val = parseInt($input.val());
                        var step = $input.attr('step');
                        step = 'undefined' !== typeof (step) ? parseInt(step) : 1;
                        if (val > 0) {
                            $input.val(val - step).change();
                        }
                    });

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
